  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">Appending
  doc: MailMerge_Appends(doc); // with key word (<SPAN style="color:#A31515">Append</SPAN>).</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">Inserting

  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">Clearing

  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">DelEmptyTableRows(doc);</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">doc.MailMerge.DeleteFields();DocumentCleanDown(doc);</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:blue">return</SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt"> doc;</SPAN></P>

  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#2B91AF">MailMerge.GetRegionForLevel(), MailMerge.MergeRegion()</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>: Once all regions
  are merged, merged any document-level data:</SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#2B91AF"></SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#2B91AF">MailMerge.MergeDocumentData()</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Finaly Remove any
  empty paragraphs:</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Select notes with </SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#A31515">&quot;//Paragraph[Run='REMOVE_PARA']&quot;</SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt"> then remove.</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</SPAN></P>
  </TD>
 </TR>
 <TR>
  <TD  width=128  valign=top style="width:96.0pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;border-top:none;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Note</SPAN></P>
  </TD>
  <TD  width=496  valign=top style="width:372.0pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</SPAN></P>
  </TD>

  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">SetMergeField(<SPAN style="color:#2B91AF">MergeField</SPAN> mergeField, <SPAN style="color:#2B91AF">DataRow</SPAN>
  rowData)</SPAN></P>
  </TD>

  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:

  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Gets merge value,
  then format the value.</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>If merge field’s type
  is </SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#A31515">&quot;Image:&quot;</SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">, then set merge field: </SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#2B91AF">MailMerge.SetImageMergeField()</SPAN></P>

  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>If merge field’s type
  is </SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#A31515">&quot;\\rtf&quot;</SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt">, then set merge field:</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:

  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Else set text merge
  field:</SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:

  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
  justify;line-height:normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US>Make sure that the
  node is either a pargraph or table: </SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:
  9.5pt"></SPAN></P>
  <P  class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
  normal"><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt;color:#2B91AF">NodeType.Paragraph</SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt"> or <SPAN style="color:#2B91AF">NodeType.Table</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
  lang=EN-US>Loop through all sections in the source document, and Loop
  through all block level nodes (paragraphs and tables) in the body of the
  section. Check to skip the node if it is a last empty paragraph in a section
  and Insert new node after the reference node.</SPAN><SPAN  lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.5pt"></SPAN></P>
  </TD>
